There is a children's activity space opposite the restaurant. We caught up with the Frozen and twisting rope handmade activities.

The room is relatively spacious, the sliding door and shower in the washroom are slightly inconvenient to operate, and the water temperature is very good.

The only drawback is that the parking space is relatively tight and the underground parking lot is relatively crowded.
